     <main class="content" itemprop="mainContentOfPage" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/Blog" role="main">
      <article class="post-7344 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail category-book category-carbohydrates category-giveaway category-past-giveaways category-pasta-carbohydrates category-recipe category-review tag-bacon tag-quick-recipe tag-spaghetti entry" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
       <header class="entry-header">
        <h1 class="entry-title" itemprop="headline">
         Spaghetti with Bacon &amp; Crispy Breadcrumbs {Recipe &amp; Cook Book Giveaway}
        </h1>
        <p class="entry-meta">
         <time class="entry-time" datetime="2015-04-12T08:37:34+00:00" itemprop="datePublished">
          April 12, 2015
         </time>
         by
         <span class="entry-author" itemprop="author" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
          <a class="entry-author-link" href="http://www.elizabethskitchendiary.co.uk/author/elizabeth/" itemprop="url" rel="author">
           <span class="entry-author-name" itemprop="name">
            Elizabeth
           </span>
          </a>
         </span>
         <span class="entry-comments-link">
          <a href="http://www.elizabethskitchendiary.co.uk/2015/04/spaghetti-with-bacon-crispy-breadcrumbs.html/#comments">
           173 Comments
          </a>
         </span>
        </p>
       </header>
       <div class="entry-content" itemprop="text">
        <input class="jpibfi" type="hidden"/>
        <p style="text-align: right;">
         <em>
          Recipe from 150 Fast &amp; Simple Recipes by Parragon Books.
         </em>
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="http://www.elizabethskitchendiary.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2015/04/spaghetti-bacon-EKD.jpg">
          <img alt="Spaghetti with Bacon &amp; Crispy Breadcrumbs" class="aligncenter wp-image-7342" height="718" src="http://www.elizabethskitchendiary.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2015/04/spaghetti-bacon-EKD.jpg" width="550"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
        </p>
        <p>
         There are times when carbohydrates are required.
        </p>
        <p>
         How about carbohydrates with bacon tossed in more crispy carbohydrates! Eee!
        </p>
        <p>
         This spaghetti with bacon and crispy breadcrumbs, ready in less than half an hour, was one of the many recipes which caught my eye from Parragons new, affordable, 150 Fast &amp; Simple recipes book, published in February 2015, andpart of Parragons brand new range 150 Recipes.
         <span id="more-7344">
         </span>
        </p>
        <p>
         The 150 Recipes series is a gorgeous new range of everyday cookbooks, featuring a wide variety of simple recipes for easy cooking.
        </p>
        <p>
         <a href="http://www.elizabethskitchendiary.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2015/04/150-Fast-Simple-Recipes.jpg">
          <img alt="150 Fast Simple Recipes" class="aligncenter size-full wp-image-7347" height="458" src="http://www.elizabethskitchendiary.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2015/04/150-Fast-Simple-Recipes.jpg" width="350"/>
         </a>
        </p>
        <p>
         Developed for those busy families who dont have a lot of time to spend preparing meals,
         <a href="http://www.parragon.com/uk/books/detail/fast-simple" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
          Fast &amp; Simple
         </a>
         is packed with 150 time-saving dishes, from light bites like Chicken and Herb Fritters and Chipotle Pork Fajitas, to more adventurous dishes, such as Steak with Chimichurri or Moroccan Meatballs with Mint Yogurt.
        </p>
        <p>
         This beautiful little book offers 150 easy-to-follow recipes, along with mouth-watering photography to entice you to experiment in the kitchen and is a concise introduction to the world of fast and simple cooking  theres no fancy ingredients or complicated techniques, just simple home cooking ready in less than 45 minutes.
        </p>
        <p>
         The book is a small 256 page hardback measuring only12 x 2.4 x 15 cm, and it is divided into seven sections:
        </p>
        <ul>
         <li>
          Introduction  featuring time saving tips
         </li>
         <li>
          Light Bites  soups, salads and starters
         </li>
         <li>
          Meat &amp; Poultry
         </li>
         <li>
          Fish &amp; Seafood
         </li>
         <li>
          Vegetarian
         </li>
         <li>
          Baking &amp; Desserts
         </li>
         <li>
          Index  a comprehensive index divided into recipe ingredients
         </li>
        </ul>
        <p>
         For a small book it certainly is packed with inspiration, and retailing at only 5.99 it would make a great addition to any kitchen. I will certainly be referring to it often!
        </p>
        <div class="wpurp-container" data-permalink="http://www.elizabethskitchendiary.co.uk/recipe/spaghetti-with-bacon-crispy-breadcrumbs/" data-servings-original="2" id="wpurp-container-recipe-7340" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Recipe" style="margin:0 auto !important;padding-top:10px !important;padding-bottom:10px !important;padding-left:10px !important;padding-right:10px !important;max-width:600px !important;position:static !important;background-color:#ebe3e2 !important;border-width:1px !important;border-color:#bbbbbb !important;border-style:solid !important;color:#444444 !important;font-family:Open Sans, sans-serif !important;">

                    <span class="wpurp-recipe-ingredient-notes recipe-ingredient-notes" style="color:#666666 !important;font-size:0.9em !important;margin-left:5px !important;">
                     chopped
                    </span>
                   </li>
                   <li class="wpurp-recipe-ingredient" itemprop="ingredients" style="line-height:1.6em !important;list-style:square !important;">
                    <span class="recipe-ingredient-quantity-unit" style="display:inline-block !important;min-width:110px !important;">
                     <span class="wpurp-recipe-ingredient-quantity recipe-ingredient-quantity" data-fraction="" data-normalized="0" data-original="">
                     </span>
                     <span class="wpurp-recipe-ingredient-unit recipe-ingredient-unit" data-original="" style="color:#666666 !important;font-size:0.9em !important;">
                     </span>
                    </span>
                    <span class="wpurp-recipe-ingredient-name recipe-ingredient-name">
                     <a href="http://www.elizabethskitchendiary.co.uk/ingredient/salt-and-pepper/" style="color: #630c0d !important;">
                      salt and pepper
                     </a>
                    </span>
                   </li>
                  </ul>
                 </div>
                 <div class="wpurp-rows-row" style="height:auto !important;">
                  <span class="wpurp-box" style="position:static !important;text-align:left !important;">
                   <span class="wpurp-title" style="margin-right:7px !important;position:static !important;text-align:left !important;">
                    Servings:
                   </span>
                   <span class="wpurp-recipe-servings-changer" style="position:static !important;text-align:left !important;">
                    <input class="advanced-adjust-recipe-servings" data-original="2" data-start-servings="2" style="width:40px !important;padding:2px !important;background:white !important;border:1px solid #bbbbbb !important;" type="number" value="2"/>
                    people
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <div class="wpurp-rows-row" style="height:auto !important;">
                  <span class="wpurp-box" style="margin-top:5px !important;position:static !important;text-align:left !important;">
                   <span class="wpurp-title" style="margin-right:5px !important;position:static !important;text-align:left !important;">
                    Units:
                   </span>
                   <span class="wpurp-recipe-unit-changer" style="position:static !important;text-align:left !important;">
                    <select class="adjust-recipe-unit" onchange="RecipeUnitConversion.recalculate(this)" style="background:white !important;border:1px solid #bbbbbb !important;">
                     <option value="0">
                      Metric
                     </option>
                     <option value="1">
                      US Imperial
                     </option>
                    </select>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                </div>
               </td>
               <td style="vertical-align:top !important;text-align:left !important;width:auto !important;">
               </td>
              </tr>
             </tbody>
            </table>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="wpurp-rows-row" style="height:auto !important;">
           <div class="wpurp-rows" style="position:static !important;text-align:left !important;">
            <div class="wpurp-rows-row" style="height:auto !important;">
             <span class="wpurp-title" style="margin-top:20px !important;margin-bottom:10px !important;position:static !important;text-align:left !important;font-weight:bold !important;font-size:1.2em !important;line-height:1.2em !important;">
              Instructions
             </span>
            </div>
            <div class="wpurp-rows-row" style="height:auto !important;">
             <ol class="wpurp-recipe-instructions" style="margin:0 23px 5px 23px !important;position:static !important;text-align:left !important;">
              <li class="wpurp-recipe-instruction" style="padding-top:5px !important;padding-bottom:15px !important;margin-bottom:10px !important;border-bottom:1px dashed #999 !important;list-style:decimal !important;">
               <span itemprop="recipeInstructions" style="vertical-align:top !important;">
                Put the bread, including any crusts, in a food processor or blender and process until the mixture resembles coarse breadcrumbs.
               </span>
              </li>
              <li class="wpurp-recipe-instruction" style="padding-top:5px !important;padding-bottom:15px !important;margin-bottom:10px !important;border-bottom:1px dashed #999 !important;list-style:decimal !important;">
               <span itemprop="recipeInstructions" style="vertical-align:top !important;">
                Bring a large saucepan of lightly salted water to the boil. Add the pasta, bring back to the boil and cook for 8-10 minutes, until tender but firm to the bite. Drain.
               </span>
              </li>
              <li class="wpurp-recipe-instruction" style="padding-top:5px !important;padding-bottom:15px !important;margin-bottom:10px !important;border-bottom:1px dashed #999 !important;list-style:decimal !important;">
               <span itemprop="recipeInstructions" style="vertical-align:top !important;">
                Meanwhile, heat the oil in a large frying pan, add the bacon and rosemary and fry for 2-3 minutes, until the bacon is golden brown. Remove from the pan with a slotted spoon and set aside.
               </span>
              </li>
              <li class="wpurp-recipe-instruction" style="padding-top:5px !important;padding-bottom:15px !important;margin-bottom:10px !important;border-bottom:1px dashed #999 !important;list-style:decimal !important;">
               <span itemprop="recipeInstructions" style="vertical-align:top !important;">
                Add the butter to the remaining bacon fat in the pan. When melted, add the breadcrumbs, pine nuts and garlic. Fry for 2-3 minutes, stirring until golden brown. Combine the breadcrumb mixture with the pasta, bacon and rosemary. Add the parsley and season to taste with pepper.
               </span>
              </li>
              <li class="wpurp-recipe-instruction" style="padding-top:5px !important;padding-bottom:15px !important;margin-bottom:10px !important;border-bottom:1px dashed #999 !important;list-style:decimal !important;border-bottom:none !important;">
               <span itemprop="recipeInstructions" style="vertical-align:top !important;">
                Transfer to warmed serving bowls and serve immediately.
               </span>
              </li>
             </ol>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="wpurp-rows-row" style="height:auto !important;">
           <div class="wpurp-rows" style="position:static !important;text-align:left !important;">
            <div class="wpurp-rows-row" style="height:auto !important;">
             <span class="wpurp-title" style="margin-top:20px !important;margin-bottom:10px !important;position:static !important;text-align:left !important;font-weight:bold !important;font-size:1.2em !important;line-height:1.2em !important;">
              Recipe Notes
             </span>
            </div>
            <div class="wpurp-rows-row" style="height:auto !important;">
             <div class="wpurp-recipe-notes" style="position:static !important;text-align:left !important;">
              <p>
               Recipe reproduced with permission from 150 Fast &amp; Simple Recipes, published by Parragon Books ISBN 978-1-4723-6348-0
              </p>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
          </div>
          <div class="wpurp-rows-row" style="height:auto !important;">

            Got a recipe for sausage cassoulet that only takes 30 minutes  have it a lot
           </p>
